<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="right">Exhibit 99.1 </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:13pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT
 COLOR="#666666">Microsoft Cloud Strength Drives Third Quarter Results </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:15pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>REDMOND, Wash. &#151; April</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;29, 2020
&#151; </B>Microsoft Corp. today announced the following results for the quarter ended March&nbsp;31, 2020, as compared to the corresponding period of last fiscal year: </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT COLOR="#666666">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Revenue was $35.0&nbsp;billion and increased 15% </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT COLOR="#666666">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Operating income was $13.0&nbsp;billion and increased 25% </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT COLOR="#666666">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Net income was $10.8&nbsp;billion and increased 22% </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT COLOR="#666666">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Diluted earnings per share was $1.40 and increased 23% </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">&#147;We&#146;ve seen two years&#146; worth of digital transformation in two months. From remote teamwork and learning, to sales and customer
service, to critical cloud infrastructure and security &#150; we are working alongside customers every day to help them adapt and stay open for business in a world of remote everything,&#148; said Satya Nadella, chief executive officer of Microsoft.
&#147;Our durable business model, diversified portfolio, and differentiated technology stack position us well for what&#146;s ahead.&#148; </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT
 COLOR="#666666">&#147;In this dynamic environment, our sales teams and partners executed a solid third quarter, with Commercial Cloud revenue generating $13.3&nbsp;billion, up 39% year over year,&#148; said Amy Hood, executive vice president and
chief financial officer of Microsoft. &#147;We remain committed to balancing operational discipline with continued investments in key strategic areas to drive future growth.&#148; </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> Impact </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">In the third quarter of fiscal year 2020, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> had minimal net impact on the total company revenue.
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">In the Productivity and Business Processes and Intelligent Cloud segments, cloud usage increased, particularly in Microsoft 365
including Teams, Azure, Windows Virtual Desktop, advanced security solutions, and Power Platform, as customers shifted to work and learn from home. In the final weeks of the quarter, there was a slowdown in transactional licensing, particularly in
small and medium businesses, and a reduction in advertising spend in LinkedIn. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">In the More Personal Computing segment, Windows OEM and
Surface benefited from increased demand to support remote work and learn scenarios, offset in part by supply chain constraints in China that improved late in the quarter. Gaming benefited from increased engagement following <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">stay-at-home</FONT></FONT> guidelines. Search was negatively impacted by reductions in advertising spend, particularly in the industries most impacted by
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19.</FONT> The effects of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> may not be fully reflected in the financial results until future periods. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>Segment Highlights </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Revenue in Productivity and Business Processes was $11.7&nbsp;billion and increased 15% (up 16% in constant currency), with the following business
highlights: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT COLOR="#666666">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Office Commercial products and cloud services revenue increased 13% (up 15% in constant currency)
driven by Office 365 Commercial revenue growth of 25% (up 27% in constant currency) </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Revenue in More Personal Computing was $11.0&nbsp;billion and increased 3% (up 4% in constant currency), with the following business highlights:
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>Return to Shareholders </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Microsoft returned $9.9&nbsp;billion to shareholders in the form of share repurchases and dividends in the third quarter of fiscal year 2020, an
increase of 33% compared to the third quarter of fiscal year 2019. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>Business Outlook </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Microsoft will provide forward-looking guidance in connection with this quarterly earnings announcement on its earnings conference call and
webcast. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>Responding to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">At Microsoft, our focus remains on ensuring the safety of our employees, striving to protect the health and well-being of the communities
in&nbsp;which we operate, and providing technology and resources to our customers and partners to help them do their best work while remote. Additional information about Microsoft&#146;s <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> response can
be found <U>here</U>. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>Quarterly Product Releases and Enhancements</B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Every quarter Microsoft delivers hundreds of products, either as new releases, services, or enhancements to current products and services. These
releases are a result of significant research and development investments, made over multiple years, designed to help customers be more productive and secure and to deliver differentiated value across the cloud and the edge. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Here are the <U>major product releases and other highlights</U> for the quarter, organized by product categories, to help illustrate how we are
accelerating innovation across our businesses while expanding our market opportunities. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>Environmental, Social, and Governance (ESG)
</B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">To better execute on Microsoft&#146;s mission, we focus our Environmental, Social, and Governance (ESG) efforts where we can have
the most positive impact. To learn more about our latest initiatives and priorities, please visit our investor relations <U>ESG website</U>.</FONT></P>
</DIV></Center>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>Webcast Details </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Satya Nadella, chief executive officer, Amy Hood, executive vice president and chief financial officer, Frank Brod, chief accounting officer,
Keith Dolliver, deputy general counsel, and Michael Spencer, general manager of investor relations, will host a conference call and webcast at 2:30 p.m. Pacific time (5:30 p.m. Eastern time) today to discuss details of the company&#146;s performance
for the quarter and certain forward-looking information. The session may be accessed at <U><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">http://www.microsoft.com/en-us/investor</FONT></U>. The webcast will be available for replay through the close of business on
April&nbsp;29, 2021. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>Constant Currency </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Microsoft presents constant currency information to provide a framework for assessing how our underlying businesses performed excluding the effect
of foreign currency rate fluctuations. To present this information, current and comparative prior period results for entities reporting in currencies other than United States dollars are converted into United States dollars using the average
exchange rates from the comparative period rather than the actual exchange rates in effect during the respective periods. All growth comparisons relate to the corresponding period in the last fiscal year. Microsoft has provided this <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial information to aid investors in better understanding our performance. The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures presented in this release should not be considered as
a substitute for, or superior to, the measures of financial performance prepared in accordance with generally accepted accounting principles (GAAP). </FONT></P>
